CREATE TABLE [dbo].[BoothMember](
	[AadharId] [bigint] NULL,
	[id] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[BoothMemberId]  AS ('BMI'+right('0000'+CONVERT([varchar](10),[id]),(10))) PERSISTED NOT NULL,
	[StateId] [int] NULL,
	[status] [bit] NULL,
	[DistrictId] [int] NULL,
	[VillageId] [int] NULL,
	[PollingDate] [datetime] NULL,
	[CreatedDate] [datetime] NULL,
	[LastModifiedDate] [datetime] NULL,
	[LastModifiedBy] [int] NULL,
	[TalukId] [int] NULL,
	[AlternateMobileNumber] [bigint] NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_BoothMemberId] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[BoothMemberId] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Sp_AddEditBoothMember]    Script Date: 3/17/2024 10:16:38 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Sp_AddEditBoothMember] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@AadharId bigint
,@StateId int
,@AlternateMobileNumber bigint
,@DistrictId int 
,@VillageId int
,@TalukId int
,@LastModifiedBy int
,@status bit
,@type char
,@boothmemberid nvarchar(13)

AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
if(@type = 'I')
  Begin -- Insert statements for procedure here
insert  [dbo].[BoothMember]
([AadharId],[StateId] ,[DistrictId],[VillageId],[CreatedDate],[LastModifiedBy],[status],[AlternateMobileNumber],[TalukId]) values 
(@AadharId
,@StateId
,@DistrictId
,@VillageId 
,getdate()
,@LastModifiedBy
,@status
,@AlternateMobileNumber
,@TalukId)

select [BoothMemberId] from [dbo].[BoothMember] where [AadharId] = @AadharId
End
else
Begin
if(@boothmemberid = '' or @boothmemberid is null)
begin
select 'Invalid Booth Member Id' 
end
else
begin
update [dbo].[BoothMember] set
AadharId = @AadharId,
StateId=@StateId,
DistrictId = @DistrictId,
VillageId = @VillageId,
LastModifiedBy = @LastModifiedBy,
[status] = @status,
AlternateMobileNumber = @AlternateMobileNumber,
TalukId = @TalukId,
LastModifiedDate = GETDATE()
where BoothMemberId = @boothmemberid
end
select [BoothMemberId] from [dbo].[BoothMember] where [AadharId] = @AadharId
End
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_GetBoothMemberByID]    Script Date: 3/17/2024 10:16:38 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetBoothMemberByID] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
	@strBoothMemberID nvarchar(10)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
select bo.[BoothMemberId] ,
aa.FirstName+' '+aa.LastName as 'BoothMemberName',
aa.MobileNumber ,
bo.[status] as 'BMstatus' ,
bo.StateId ,
bo.DistrictId ,
bo.TalukId ,
bo.VillageId ,
bo.PollingDate ,
bo.AlternateMobileNumber 
from [dbo].[BoothMember] as bo 
join [dbo].[Aadhar] as 
aa on aa.AadharId = bo.AadharId
where bo.[BoothMemberId] = @strBoothMemberID
	END




GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_GetVoterDetailsByID]    Script Date: 3/17/2024 10:16:38 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetVoterDetailsByID] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
	@strEnRollID bigint,
	@VoterID nvarchar(12)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	if(@strEnRollID >0 )
	
	select vd.AadharId,vd.VoterStatus, aa.FirstName +' '+ aa.LastName as VoterName from VoterDetails vd join Aadhar aa 
	on vd.AadharId = aa.AadharId
	where vd.EnrollmentId = @strEnRollID

	else

	select vd.AadharId,vd.VoterStatus, aa.FirstName +' '+ aa.LastName as VoterName from VoterDetails vd join Aadhar aa 
	on vd.AadharId = aa.AadharId
	where vd.VoterID = @VoterID

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
	
END
GO

CREATE   PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_PartyName] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
	 @VillageId int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
select pai.PartyName,pai.PartyId
from 
dbo.PartyIdList as plist join dbo.Party as pai on pai.PartyId = plist.PartyId
where plist.VillageId = @VillageId
END

-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_VerifyBMLoginDetails]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
	@BMID nvarchar(10),
	@AAID nvarchar(12)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	declare @strID int
	select @strID = [id] from [BoothMember] where [BoothMemberId] = @BMID and [AadharId] = @AAID
    -- Insert statements for procedure here
	if(@strID='' or @strID is null)
	begin
	select 0
	end
	else
	begin
	select @strID
	end

END
GO

	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here

    -- Insert statements for procedure here

	begin
	select 0
	end
	else
	begin
	select @strID
	end

END

create procedure [dbo].[st_altertable] @in varchar(1) 
as
begin
if 'A'=@in
alter table [dbo].[DEC] 
alter column [LastModifiedBy] varchar(10);

else 
update [dbo].[DEC] set [LastModifiedBy] ='DECID01';
end 
GO

GO

GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ST_District]  @DecId int,@StateId int,@DistrictId int
	AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
	select COUNT(*) from [dbo].[DEC]
where 
DecId = @DecId
and 
StateId = @StateId 
and 
DistrictId = @DistrictId
END
GO
